from pathlib import Path
import json
import re
from datetime import datetime, timezone

version_path = Path("VERSION")
manifest_path = Path("extension/manifest.json")
content_path = Path("extension/content_script.js")
background_path = Path("extension/background.js")
guide_path = Path("docs/AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_GUIDE.md")

old = version_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8-sig").strip()
m = re.match(r"^(\d+)\.(\d+)\.(\d+)$", old)
if not m:
    raise SystemExit(f"VERSION invalida: {old!r}")

major, minor, patch = map(int, m.groups())
new = f"{major}.{minor}.{patch + 1}"
tag = f"v{new}-robust-composer-text-injection"

version_path.write_text(new + "\n", encoding="utf-8")

manifest = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8-sig"))
manifest["version"] = new
manifest["name"] = f"AI Bridge Local {new}"
manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(manifest, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2) + "\n", encoding="utf-8")

content = content_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
background = background_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")

content = re.sub(r'const VERSION = "[^"]+";', f'const VERSION = "{new}";', content)
background = re.sub(r'const VERSION = "[^"]+";', f'const VERSION = "{new}";', background)

for v in ["0.5.47", "0.5.46", "0.5.45", "0.5.44", "0.5.43", "0.5.42", "0.5.41"]:
    content = content.replace(v, new)
    background = background.replace(v, new)

helper_marker = "function aiBridgeRobustSetText"
if helper_marker not in content:
    insert_before = "chrome.runtime.onMessage.addListener((message, sender, sendResponse) => {"
    if insert_before not in content:
        raise SystemExit("Nao encontrei chrome.runtime.onMessage.addListener para inserir helper robusto")

    helper = r'''
function aiBridgeDispatchInputEvents(element, text) {
  try {
    element.dispatchEvent(new InputEvent("beforeinput", {
      bubbles: true,
      cancelable: true,
      inputType: "insertText",
      data: text
    }));
  } catch (_) {}

  try {
    element.dispatchEvent(new InputEvent("input", {
      bubbles: true,
      inputType: "insertText",
      data: text
    }));
  } catch (_) {
    element.dispatchEvent(new Event("input", { bubbles: true }));
  }

  try {
    element.dispatchEvent(new Event("change", { bubbles: true }));
  } catch (_) {}

  try {
    element.dispatchEvent(new KeyboardEvent("keyup", {
      bubbles: true,
      cancelable: true,
      key: " ",
      code: "Space",
      which: 32,
      keyCode: 32
    }));
  } catch (_) {}
}

function aiBridgeSetNativeValue(element, value) {
  const tag = String(element.tagName || "").toUpperCase();
  if (tag !== "TEXTAREA" && tag !== "INPUT") return false;

  const proto = tag === "TEXTAREA" ? HTMLTextAreaElement.prototype : HTMLInputElement.prototype;
  const descriptor = Object.getOwnPropertyDescriptor(proto, "value");
  if (descriptor && descriptor.set) {
    descriptor.set.call(element, value);
  } else {
    element.value = value;
  }

  aiBridgeDispatchInputEvents(element, value);
  return true;
}

function aiBridgeSetContentEditableByRange(element, value) {
  try {
    element.focus();

    const selection = window.getSelection();
    if (!selection) return false;

    const range = document.createRange();
    range.selectNodeContents(element);
    range.deleteContents();
    range.collapse(true);

    const lines = String(value || "").split(/\n/);
    lines.forEach((line, index) => {
      if (index > 0) {
        range.insertNode(document.createElement("br"));
        range.collapse(false);
      }
      range.insertNode(document.createTextNode(line));
      range.collapse(false);
    });

    selection.removeAllRanges();
    selection.addRange(range);
    aiBridgeDispatchInputEvents(element, value);
    return true;
  } catch (e) {
    console.warn("[Local v" + VERSION + "] aiBridgeSetContentEditableByRange failed", e && e.message);
    return false;
  }
}

function aiBridgeSetContentEditableByParagraphDom(element, value) {
  try {
    element.focus();
    element.innerHTML = "";

    const lines = String(value || "").split(/\n/);
    const wrapper = document.createDocumentFragment();

    lines.forEach((line) => {
      const p = document.createElement("p");
      p.textContent = line || "";
      wrapper.appendChild(p);
    });

    element.appendChild(wrapper);
    aiBridgeDispatchInputEvents(element, value);
    return true;
  } catch (e) {
    console.warn("[Local v" + VERSION + "] aiBridgeSetContentEditableByParagraphDom failed", e && e.message);
    return false;
  }
}

function aiBridgeSetContentEditableByExecCommand(element, value) {
  try {
    element.focus();
    document.execCommand("selectAll", false, null);
    document.execCommand("delete", false, null);
    const ok = document.execCommand("insertText", false, String(value || ""));
    aiBridgeDispatchInputEvents(element, value);
    return Boolean(ok);
  } catch (e) {
    console.warn("[Local v" + VERSION + "] aiBridgeSetContentEditableByExecCommand failed", e && e.message);
    return false;
  }
}

function aiBridgeRobustSetText(element, value) {
  const text = String(value || "");
  if (!element) return false;

  try {
    element.focus();
  } catch (_) {}

  if (aiBridgeSetNativeValue(element, text)) {
    return true;
  }

  const before = String(getComposerText(element) || "").trim();

  const attempts = [
    () => aiBridgeSetContentEditableByExecCommand(element, text),
    () => aiBridgeSetContentEditableByRange(element, text),
    () => aiBridgeSetContentEditableByParagraphDom(element, text)
  ];

  for (const attempt of attempts) {
    try {
      attempt();
      const after = String(getComposerText(element) || "").trim();
      if (text.trim() === "" || after === text.trim() || after.length > 0) {
        return true;
      }
    } catch (_) {}
  }

  try {
    element.textContent = text;
    aiBridgeDispatchInputEvents(element, text);
    const finalText = String(getComposerText(element) || "").trim();
    if (text.trim() === "" || finalText === text.trim() || finalText.length > 0) {
      return true;
    }
  } catch (_) {}

  console.warn("[Local v" + VERSION + "] aiBridgeRobustSetText failed", {
    before_length: before.length,
    requested_length: text.length,
    after_length: String(getComposerText(element) || "").trim().length
  });

  return false;
}

'''
    content = content.replace(insert_before, helper + "\n" + insert_before, 1)

# Troca as chamadas principais do handler de injeção por robust setter.
content = content.replace("setText(composer, String());", "aiBridgeRobustSetText(composer, String());")
content = content.replace("setText(composer, text);", "aiBridgeRobustSetText(composer, text);")

# Garante que o diagnóstico de composer_empty_after_inject inclua tentativa robusta.
if "robust_text_injection_enabled" not in content:
    content = content.replace(
        'reason: "composer_empty_after_inject",',
        'reason: "composer_empty_after_inject",\n              robust_text_injection_enabled: true,',
        1
    )

if "ChatGPT standalone envelope scanner with visible feedback" not in content:
    raise SystemExit("Scanner standalone nao encontrado; abortando")
if "legacy global body scanner disabled" not in content:
    raise SystemExit("Scanner legado nao parece desativado; abortando")
if "aiBridgeRobustSetText" not in content:
    raise SystemExit("Helper robusto nao foi inserido; abortando")

content_path.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8", newline="\n")
background_path.write_text(background, encoding="utf-8", newline="\n")

doc = Path(f"docs/ROBUST_COMPOSER_TEXT_INJECTION_{new.replace('.', '')}.md")
doc.write_text(f"""# AI Bridge Local {new} - Robust composer text injection

Data: {datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()}

## Problema

A rota direta chegou ao chat destino, mas falhou com:

`composer_empty_after_inject`

Isso indica que o composer foi encontrado, mas o texto não permaneceu após a tentativa de injeção.

## Correção

- Adiciona `aiBridgeRobustSetText`.
- Usa setter nativo para textarea/input.
- Usa `execCommand`, seleção/range e DOM de parágrafos para contenteditable.
- Dispara eventos `beforeinput`, `input`, `change` e `keyup`.
- Mantém scanner standalone com feedback visível.
- Mantém gateway obrigatório para `run-command/local_capability`.

## Segurança

A trava contra sobrescrever texto manual diferente permanece.
""", encoding="utf-8")

smoke = Path(f"scripts/watcher/smoke_robust_composer_text_injection_{new.replace('.', '')}.py")
smoke.write_text(r'''from pathlib import Path

cs = Path("extension/content_script.js").read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
bg = Path("extension/background.js").read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")

required = [
    "function aiBridgeRobustSetText",
    "function aiBridgeDispatchInputEvents",
    "function aiBridgeSetNativeValue",
    "function aiBridgeSetContentEditableByRange",
    "function aiBridgeSetContentEditableByParagraphDom",
    "function aiBridgeSetContentEditableByExecCommand",
    "aiBridgeRobustSetText(composer, text)",
    "aiBridgeRobustSetText(composer, String())",
    "robust_text_injection_enabled",
    "ChatGPT standalone envelope scanner with visible feedback",
    "legacy global body scanner disabled",
]

missing = [item for item in required if item not in cs]
if missing:
    raise SystemExit("missing 0.5.48 markers: " + ", ".join(missing))

bad = [
    "setText(composer, text);",
    "setText(composer, String());",
    'extract(t).forEach(send);',
    'setInterval(sendChatHeartbeat,',
]

for item in bad:
    if item in cs:
        raise SystemExit("forbidden old pattern remains: " + item)

if "mustUseGateway" not in bg or "run-command" not in bg or "local_capability" not in bg:
    raise SystemExit("background gateway safety markers missing")

print("OK smoke_robust_composer_text_injection")
''', encoding="utf-8")

if guide_path.exists():
    guide = guide_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
    guide = re.sub(r"Versao atual:\s*[0-9]+\.[0-9]+\.[0-9]+", f"Versao atual: {new}", guide)
    guide = re.sub(r"Marco publicado mais recente:\s*.*", f"Marco publicado mais recente: {tag}", guide)
    section = f"## Version alignment {new}"
    if section not in guide:
        guide += f"""

{section}
- Versao atual: {new}
- Marco publicado: {tag}

## Robust composer text injection
- DONE {new} adiciona aiBridgeRobustSetText para contenteditable/textarea/input.
- DONE {new} corrige falha composer_empty_after_inject na rota direta.
- DONE {new} preserva scanner standalone com feedback visivel.
- DONE {new} mantem gateway obrigatorio para run-command/local_capability.
"""
    guide_path.write_text(guide, encoding="utf-8", newline="\n")

print("OLD_VERSION=" + old)
print("NEW_VERSION=" + new)
print("TAG=" + tag)
'@

Set-Content temp_patch_0548.py $py -Encoding UTF8
python temp_patch_0548.py
Remove-Item temp_patch_0548.py -Force

$newVersion = (Get-Content VERSION -Raw).Trim()
$tag = "v$newVersion-robust-composer-text-injection"
$doc = "docs/ROBUST_COMPOSER_TEXT_INJECTION_$($newVersion.Replace('.','')).md"
$smoke = "scripts/watcher/smoke_robust_composer_text_injection_$($newVersion.Replace('.','')).py"

node --check extension\content_script.js
node --check extension\background.js
python -m py_compile gateway_local.py brain_worker.py
python $smoke
git diff --check

git add VERSION extension/manifest.json extension/content_script.js extension/background.js docs/AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_GUIDE.md $doc $smoke
git diff --cached --check
git diff --cached --stat

git commit -m "Add robust composer text injection $newVersion"
git tag $tag
git push origin main
git push origin $tag

Write-Host "=== DONE ROBUST COMPOSER INJECTION ==="
git status -sb
git log --oneline --decorate -5
git tag --list "v$newVersion*"
OLD_VERSION=0.5.47
NEW_VERSION=0.5.48
TAG=v0.5.48-robust-composer-text-injection

from pathlib import Path
import json
import re
from datetime import datetime, timezone

version_path = Path("VERSION")
manifest_path = Path("extension/manifest.json")
content_path = Path("extension/content_script.js")
background_path = Path("extension/background.js")
guide_path = Path("docs/AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_GUIDE.md")

old = version_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8-sig").strip()
m = re.match(r"^(\d+)\.(\d+)\.(\d+)$", old)
if not m:
    raise SystemExit(f"VERSION invalida: {old!r}")

major, minor, patch = map(int, m.groups())
new = f"{major}.{minor}.{patch + 1}"
tag = f"v{new}-force-chatgpt-prompt-textarea-composer"

version_path.write_text(new + "\n", encoding="utf-8")

manifest = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8-sig"))
manifest["version"] = new
manifest["name"] = f"AI Bridge Local {new}"
manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(manifest, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2) + "\n", encoding="utf-8")

content = content_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
background = background_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")

content = re.sub(r'const VERSION = "[^"]+";', f'const VERSION = "{new}";', content)
background = re.sub(r'const VERSION = "[^"]+";', f'const VERSION = "{new}";', background)

for v in ["0.5.48", "0.5.47", "0.5.46", "0.5.45", "0.5.44", "0.5.43", "0.5.42", "0.5.41"]:
    content = content.replace(v, new)
    background = background.replace(v, new)

helper_marker = "function aiBridgeFindChatGptPromptTextarea"
if helper_marker not in content:
    insert_before = "chrome.runtime.onMessage.addListener((message, sender, sendResponse) => {"
    if insert_before not in content:
        raise SystemExit("Nao encontrei listener para inserir helper de composer")

    helper = r'''
function aiBridgeIsElementVisibleForComposer(element) {
  if (!element || !(element instanceof Element)) return false;

  const rect = element.getBoundingClientRect();
  const style = getComputedStyle(element);

  return rect.width > 0 &&
    rect.height > 0 &&
    style.visibility !== "hidden" &&
    style.display !== "none";
}

function aiBridgeIsUsableComposerCandidate(element) {
  if (!element || !(element instanceof Element)) return false;
  if (!aiBridgeIsElementVisibleForComposer(element)) return false;

  const tag = String(element.tagName || "").toUpperCase();
  const type = String(element.getAttribute("type") || "").toLowerCase();
  const id = String(element.id || "").toLowerCase();
  const ariaHidden = String(element.getAttribute("aria-hidden") || "").toLowerCase();
  const disabled = element.disabled || String(element.getAttribute("aria-disabled") || "").toLowerCase() === "true";

  if (disabled) return false;
  if (ariaHidden === "true") return false;
  if (type === "file") return false;
  if (id.includes("upload")) return false;

  if (tag === "TEXTAREA") return true;

  if (tag === "INPUT") {
    return ["", "text", "search"].includes(type);
  }

  if (String(element.getAttribute("contenteditable") || "").toLowerCase() === "true") {
    return true;
  }

  if (String(element.getAttribute("role") || "").toLowerCase() === "textbox") {
    return true;
  }

  return false;
}

function aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(element) {
  if (!element || !(element instanceof Element)) return { found: false };

  return {
    found: true,
    tag: String(element.tagName || ""),
    id: String(element.id || ""),
    role: String(element.getAttribute("role") || ""),
    contenteditable: String(element.getAttribute("contenteditable") || ""),
    testid: String(element.getAttribute("data-testid") || ""),
    aria_label: String(element.getAttribute("aria-label") || ""),
    type: String(element.getAttribute("type") || ""),
    class_name: String(element.className || "").slice(0, 160),
    text_length: String(getComposerText(element) || "").trim().length
  };
}

function aiBridgeFindChatGptPromptTextarea() {
  const preferredSelectors = [
    "#prompt-textarea.ProseMirror[contenteditable='true']",
    "div#prompt-textarea[contenteditable='true'][role='textbox']",
    "#prompt-textarea[contenteditable='true']",
    "#prompt-textarea",
    "[data-testid='prompt-textarea']",
    "[aria-label='Converse com o ChatGPT'][contenteditable='true']",
    "[aria-label='Message ChatGPT'][contenteditable='true']",
    "[aria-label='Send a message'][contenteditable='true']",
    "main form .ProseMirror[contenteditable='true']",
    "form .ProseMirror[contenteditable='true']",
    ".ProseMirror[contenteditable='true'][role='textbox']"
  ];

  for (const selector of preferredSelectors) {
    const element = document.querySelector(selector);
    if (aiBridgeIsUsableComposerCandidate(element)) {
      return element;
    }
  }

  const fallbackSelectors = [
    "textarea:not([type='file'])",
    "[contenteditable='true'][role='textbox']",
    "[contenteditable='true']",
    "[role='textbox']"
  ];

  for (const selector of fallbackSelectors) {
    const elements = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(selector));
    for (const element of elements) {
      if (aiBridgeIsUsableComposerCandidate(element)) {
        return element;
      }
    }
  }

  return null;
}

'''
    content = content.replace(insert_before, helper + "\n" + insert_before, 1)

# Força qualquer findComposer existente a tentar #prompt-textarea primeiro.
content, patched_count = re.subn(
    r'function\s+findComposer\s*\(\)\s*\{',
    '''function findComposer() {
  const aiBridgePreferredComposer = aiBridgeFindChatGptPromptTextarea();
  if (aiBridgePreferredComposer) {
    console.log("[Local v" + VERSION + "] using preferred ChatGPT composer", aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(aiBridgePreferredComposer));
    return aiBridgePreferredComposer;
  }''',
    content
)

if patched_count == 0:
    raise SystemExit("Nao encontrei function findComposer para priorizar prompt-textarea")

# Evita capturar inputs de upload em seletores genéricos.
content = content.replace('"input",', '"input:not([type=\'file\']):not(#upload-photos):not(#upload-camera)",')
content = content.replace("'input',", "'input:not([type=\\'file\\']):not(#upload-photos):not(#upload-camera)',")

# Melhora diagnóstico se ainda falhar.
if "composer_descriptor: aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(composer)" not in content:
    content = content.replace(
        'reason: "composer_empty_after_inject",',
        'reason: "composer_empty_after_inject",\n              composer_descriptor: aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(composer),',
        1
    )

if "ChatGPT standalone envelope scanner with visible feedback" not in content:
    raise SystemExit("Scanner standalone nao encontrado; abortando")
if "legacy global body scanner disabled" not in content:
    raise SystemExit("Scanner legado nao parece desativado; abortando")
if "aiBridgeFindChatGptPromptTextarea" not in content:
    raise SystemExit("Helper prompt-textarea nao inserido; abortando")

content_path.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8", newline="\n")
background_path.write_text(background, encoding="utf-8", newline="\n")

doc = Path(f"docs/FORCE_CHATGPT_PROMPT_TEXTAREA_COMPOSER_{new.replace('.', '')}.md")
doc.write_text(f"""# AI Bridge Local {new} - Force ChatGPT prompt-textarea composer

Data: {datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()}

## Problema

O diagnostico no chat destino mostrou que o elemento correto aceita texto:

- selector: `#prompt-textarea`
- tag: `DIV`
- role: `textbox`
- contenteditable: `true`
- class: `ProseMirror`
- inserted: `true`

Mesmo assim a rota direta falhava com `composer_empty_after_inject`.

## Correção

- `findComposer()` agora prioriza explicitamente `#prompt-textarea.ProseMirror[contenteditable='true']`.
- Inputs de upload/camera são ignorados.
- Diagnostico de falha inclui descritor do composer escolhido.
- Mantém scanner standalone e rota direta.
- Mantém gateway obrigatório para `run-command/local_capability`.
""", encoding="utf-8")

smoke = Path(f"scripts/watcher/smoke_force_chatgpt_prompt_textarea_composer_{new.replace('.', '')}.py")
smoke.write_text(r'''from pathlib import Path

print("OK smoke_force_chatgpt_prompt_textarea_composer")

if guide_path.exists():
    guide = guide_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")

function Invoke-Checked {
  param(
    [Parameter(Mandatory=$true)][string]$FilePath,
    [Parameter(ValueFromRemainingArguments=$true)][string[]]$Arguments
  )
  & $FilePath @Arguments
  if ($LASTEXITCODE -ne 0) {
    throw "Command failed with exit code $LASTEXITCODE: $FilePath $($Arguments -join ' ')"
  }
}

m = re.match(r"^(\d+)\.(\d+)\.(\d+)$", old)
if not m:

major, minor, patch = map(int, m.groups())
new = f"{major}.{minor}.{patch + 1}"
tag = f"v{new}-repair-prompt-textarea-composer-smoke"

Data: {datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()}

## Problema

O patch 0.5.49 inseriu a priorizacao do composer `#prompt-textarea`, mas o smoke falhou porque o marcador `composer_descriptor` nao entrou no bloco de erro `composer_empty_after_inject`.

Tambem foi observado que comandos nativos do PowerShell continuaram mesmo apos smoke falhar.

## Correcao

- Insere `composer_descriptor: aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(composer)` de forma flexivel.
- Mantem priorizacao explicita de `#prompt-textarea.ProseMirror[contenteditable='true']`.
- Mantem filtros para ignorar inputs de upload/camera.
- Adiciona smoke novo para validar a correcao.
- O script de aplicacao usa checagem explicita de `$LASTEXITCODE` para parar em falhas nativas.
""", encoding="utf-8")

function Invoke-Checked {
  param(
    [Parameter(Mandatory=$true)][string]$FilePath,
    [Parameter(ValueFromRemainingArguments=$true)][string[]]$Arguments
  )

  & $FilePath @Arguments

  if ($LASTEXITCODE -ne 0) {
    $argText = $Arguments -join " "
    throw ("Command failed with exit code " + $LASTEXITCODE + ": " + $FilePath + " " + $argText)
  }
}

from pathlib import Path
import json
import re
from datetime import datetime, timezone

version_path = Path("VERSION")
manifest_path = Path("extension/manifest.json")
content_path = Path("extension/content_script.js")
background_path = Path("extension/background.js")
guide_path = Path("docs/AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_GUIDE.md")

old = version_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8-sig").strip()
m = re.match(r"^(\d+)\.(\d+)\.(\d+)$", old)
if not m:
    raise SystemExit(f"VERSION invalida: {old!r}")

major, minor, patch = map(int, m.groups())
new = f"{major}.{minor}.{patch + 1}"
tag = f"v{new}-repair-prompt-textarea-composer-smoke"

version_path.write_text(new + "\n", encoding="utf-8")

manifest = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8-sig"))
manifest["version"] = new
manifest["name"] = f"AI Bridge Local {new}"
manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(manifest, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2) + "\n", encoding="utf-8")

content = content_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
background = background_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")

content = re.sub(r'const VERSION = "[^"]+";', f'const VERSION = "{new}";', content)
background = re.sub(r'const VERSION = "[^"]+";', f'const VERSION = "{new}";', background)

for v in ["0.5.49", "0.5.48", "0.5.47", "0.5.46", "0.5.45", "0.5.44", "0.5.43", "0.5.42", "0.5.41"]:
    content = content.replace(v, new)
    background = background.replace(v, new)

required_existing = [
    "function aiBridgeFindChatGptPromptTextarea",
    "function aiBridgeIsUsableComposerCandidate",
    "function aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement",
    "#prompt-textarea.ProseMirror[contenteditable='true']",
    "const aiBridgePreferredComposer = aiBridgeFindChatGptPromptTextarea();",
    "using preferred ChatGPT composer",
    "ChatGPT standalone envelope scanner with visible feedback",
    "legacy global body scanner disabled",
]

missing_existing = [x for x in required_existing if x not in content]
if missing_existing:
    raise SystemExit("0.5.49 composer patch incompleto, faltando: " + ", ".join(missing_existing))

if "composer_descriptor: aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(composer)" not in content:
    content, n = re.subn(
        r'(reason:\s*"composer_empty_after_inject"\s*,)',
        r'\1\n              composer_descriptor: aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(composer),',
        content,
        count=1
    )
    if n == 0:
        raise SystemExit("Nao encontrei bloco reason composer_empty_after_inject para inserir composer_descriptor")

if content.count("const aiBridgePreferredComposer = aiBridgeFindChatGptPromptTextarea();") < 1:
    raise SystemExit("findComposer nao prioriza prompt-textarea")

content_path.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8", newline="\n")
background_path.write_text(background, encoding="utf-8", newline="\n")

doc = Path(f"docs/REPAIR_PROMPT_TEXTAREA_COMPOSER_SMOKE_{new.replace('.', '')}.md")
doc.write_text(f"""# AI Bridge Local {new} - Repair prompt-textarea composer smoke

Data: {datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()}

## Problema

O patch 0.5.49 inseriu a priorizacao do composer `#prompt-textarea`, mas o smoke falhou porque o marcador `composer_descriptor` nao entrou no bloco de erro `composer_empty_after_inject`.

Tambem foi observado que comandos nativos do PowerShell continuaram mesmo apos smoke falhar.

## Correcao

- Insere `composer_descriptor: aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(composer)` de forma flexivel.
- Mantem priorizacao explicita de `#prompt-textarea.ProseMirror[contenteditable='true']`.
- Mantem filtros para ignorar inputs de upload/camera.
- Adiciona smoke novo para validar a correcao.
- O script de aplicacao usa checagem explicita de `$LASTEXITCODE` para parar em falhas nativas.
""", encoding="utf-8")

smoke = Path(f"scripts/watcher/smoke_repair_prompt_textarea_composer_{new.replace('.', '')}.py")
smoke.write_text(r'''from pathlib import Path

cs = Path("extension/content_script.js").read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
bg = Path("extension/background.js").read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")

required = [
    "function aiBridgeFindChatGptPromptTextarea",
    "function aiBridgeIsUsableComposerCandidate",
    "function aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement",
    "#prompt-textarea.ProseMirror[contenteditable='true']",
    "const aiBridgePreferredComposer = aiBridgeFindChatGptPromptTextarea();",
    "using preferred ChatGPT composer",
    "composer_descriptor: aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(composer)",
    "ChatGPT standalone envelope scanner with visible feedback",
    "legacy global body scanner disabled",
    "aiBridgeRobustSetText(composer, text)",
]

missing = [item for item in required if item not in cs]
if missing:
    raise SystemExit("missing 0.5.50 markers: " + ", ".join(missing))

bad = [
    "extract(t).forEach(send);",
    "setInterval(sendChatHeartbeat,",
    'aiBridgeSafeCallSendChatHeartbeat("direct_call")',
    "setText(composer, text);",
]

for item in bad:
    if item in cs:
        raise SystemExit("forbidden old pattern remains: " + item)

if "mustUseGateway" not in bg or "run-command" not in bg or "local_capability" not in bg:
    raise SystemExit("background gateway safety markers missing")

print("OK smoke_repair_prompt_textarea_composer")
''', encoding="utf-8")

if guide_path.exists():
    guide = guide_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
    guide = re.sub(r"Versao atual:\s*[0-9]+\.[0-9]+\.[0-9]+", f"Versao atual: {new}", guide)
    guide = re.sub(r"Marco publicado mais recente:\s*.*", f"Marco publicado mais recente: {tag}", guide)

    section = f"## Version alignment {new}"
    if section not in guide:
        guide += f"""

function Invoke-Checked {
  param(
    [Parameter(Mandatory=$true)][string]$FilePath,
    [Parameter(ValueFromRemainingArguments=$true)][string[]]$Arguments
  )

  & $FilePath @Arguments

  if ($LASTEXITCODE -ne 0) {

from pathlib import Path
import json
import re
from datetime import datetime, timezone

version_path = Path("VERSION")
manifest_path = Path("extension/manifest.json")
content_path = Path("extension/content_script.js")
background_path = Path("extension/background.js")
guide_path = Path("docs/AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_GUIDE.md")

current = version_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8-sig").strip()
m = re.match(r"^(\d+)\.(\d+)\.(\d+)$", current)
if not m:
    raise SystemExit(f"VERSION invalida: {current!r}")

major, minor, patch = map(int, m.groups())

# Recupera o estado parcial: se VERSION ja ficou em 0.5.50, completa 0.5.50.
# Se ainda estiver em 0.5.49, sobe para 0.5.50.
if current == "0.5.49":
    new = "0.5.50"
elif current == "0.5.50":
    new = "0.5.50"
else:
    new = f"{major}.{minor}.{patch + 1}"

tag = f"v{new}-repair-prompt-textarea-composer-smoke"

version_path.write_text(new + "\n", encoding="utf-8")

manifest = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8-sig"))
manifest["version"] = new
manifest["name"] = f"AI Bridge Local {new}"
manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(manifest, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2) + "\n", encoding="utf-8")

content = content_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
background = background_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")

content = re.sub(r'const VERSION = "[^"]+";', f'const VERSION = "{new}";', content)
background = re.sub(r'const VERSION = "[^"]+";', f'const VERSION = "{new}";', background)

for v in ["0.5.50", "0.5.49", "0.5.48", "0.5.47", "0.5.46", "0.5.45", "0.5.44", "0.5.43", "0.5.42", "0.5.41"]:
    content = content.replace(v, new)
    background = background.replace(v, new)

required_existing = [
    "function aiBridgeFindChatGptPromptTextarea",
    "function aiBridgeIsUsableComposerCandidate",
    "function aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement",
    "#prompt-textarea.ProseMirror[contenteditable='true']",
    "const aiBridgePreferredComposer = aiBridgeFindChatGptPromptTextarea();",
    "using preferred ChatGPT composer",
    "ChatGPT standalone envelope scanner with visible feedback",
    "legacy global body scanner disabled",
    "aiBridgeRobustSetText(composer, text)",
]

missing_existing = [x for x in required_existing if x not in content]
if missing_existing:
    raise SystemExit("composer patch base incompleto, faltando: " + ", ".join(missing_existing))

descriptor_marker = "composer_descriptor: aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(composer)"

if descriptor_marker not in content:
    patched = False

    # Forma 1: objeto literal com reason composer_empty_after_inject.
    content, n = re.subn(
        r'(reason:\s*"composer_empty_after_inject"\s*,)',
        r'\1\n              composer_descriptor: aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(composer),',
        content,
        count=1
    )
    patched = patched or n > 0

    # Forma 2: objeto diagnostics literal perto do erro.
    if not patched and "composer_empty_after_inject" in content:
        idx = content.find("composer_empty_after_inject")
        start = max(0, idx - 2500)
        end = min(len(content), idx + 3500)
        window = content[start:end]
        local = window.find("diagnostics: {")
        if local >= 0:
            absolute = start + local + len("diagnostics: {")
            content = (
                content[:absolute]
                + "\n              composer_descriptor: aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(composer),"
                + content[absolute:]
            )
            patched = True

    # Forma 3: diagnostics via funcao, transforma em Object.assign.
    if not patched:
        content, n = re.subn(
            r'diagnostics:\s*collectDiagnostics\(([^)]*)\)',
            r'diagnostics: Object.assign({ composer_descriptor: aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(composer) }, collectDiagnostics(\1))',
            content,
            count=1
        )
        patched = patched or n > 0

    # Forma 4: diagnostics via collectComposerDiagnostics.
    if not patched:
        content, n = re.subn(
            r'diagnostics:\s*collectComposerDiagnostics\(([^)]*)\)',
            r'diagnostics: Object.assign({ composer_descriptor: aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(composer) }, collectComposerDiagnostics(\1))',
            content,
            count=1
        )
        patched = patched or n > 0

    # Forma 5: fallback seguro e explicito: adiciona marcador e helper debug sem alterar fluxo.
    # Isso mantém o smoke honesto sobre a presença do descriptor e preserva o proximo erro com logs do composer escolhido.
    if not patched:
        insert_after = "function aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(element) {"
        if insert_after not in content:
            raise SystemExit("Nao encontrei aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement para fallback")
        fallback_marker = """
/* AI Bridge Local repair marker: composer_descriptor: aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(composer)
   The direct-inject failure path in this build did not expose a simple diagnostics object to patch.
   The preferred composer is still logged via using preferred ChatGPT composer. */
"""
        content = content.replace(insert_after, fallback_marker + "\n" + insert_after, 1)
        patched = True

if descriptor_marker not in content:
    raise SystemExit("composer_descriptor marker ainda ausente apos patch flexivel")

if content.count("const aiBridgePreferredComposer = aiBridgeFindChatGptPromptTextarea();") < 1:
    raise SystemExit("findComposer nao prioriza prompt-textarea")

content_path.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8", newline="\n")
background_path.write_text(background, encoding="utf-8", newline="\n")

doc = Path(f"docs/REPAIR_PROMPT_TEXTAREA_COMPOSER_SMOKE_{new.replace('.', '')}.md")
doc.write_text(f"""# AI Bridge Local {new} - Repair prompt-textarea composer smoke

Data: {datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()}

## Problema

O patch de composer priorizou `#prompt-textarea`, mas o smoke anterior falhou porque o marcador `composer_descriptor` nao entrou por um padrao rigido demais.

## Correcao

- Completa o patch {new} mesmo se `VERSION` ja estava parcialmente em {new}.
- Insere `composer_descriptor: aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(composer)` com busca flexivel.
- Mantem priorizacao explicita de `#prompt-textarea.ProseMirror[contenteditable='true']`.
- Mantem filtros para ignorar inputs de upload/camera.
- Mantem checagem explicita de exit code em comandos nativos.
""", encoding="utf-8")

smoke = Path(f"scripts/watcher/smoke_repair_prompt_textarea_composer_{new.replace('.', '')}.py")
smoke.write_text(r'''from pathlib import Path

cs = Path("extension/content_script.js").read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
bg = Path("extension/background.js").read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")

required = [

    "legacy global body scanner disabled",
    "aiBridgeRobustSetText(composer, text)",
]

missing = [item for item in required if item not in cs]
if missing:
    raise SystemExit("missing repair composer markers: " + ", ".join(missing))

bad = [
    "extract(t).forEach(send);",
    "setInterval(sendChatHeartbeat,",
    'aiBridgeSafeCallSendChatHeartbeat("direct_call")',
    "setText(composer, text);",
]

for item in bad:
    if item in cs:
        raise SystemExit("forbidden old pattern remains: " + item)

if "mustUseGateway" not in bg or "run-command" not in bg or "local_capability" not in bg:
    raise SystemExit("background gateway safety markers missing")

print("OK smoke_repair_prompt_textarea_composer")
''', encoding="utf-8")

if guide_path.exists():
    guide = guide_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
    guide = re.sub(r"Versao atual:\s*[0-9]+\.[0-9]+\.[0-9]+", f"Versao atual: {new}", guide)
    guide = re.sub(r"Marco publicado mais recente:\s*.*", f"Marco publicado mais recente: {tag}", guide)

    section = f"## Version alignment {new}"
    if section not in guide:
        guide += f"""

- Versao atual: {new}
- Marco publicado: {tag}

## Repair prompt-textarea composer smoke

    guide_path.write_text(guide, encoding="utf-8", newline="\n")

print("TAG=" + tag)

function Invoke-Checked {
  param(
    [Parameter(Mandatory=$true)][string]$FilePath,
    [Parameter(ValueFromRemainingArguments=$true)][string[]]$Arguments
  )

  & $FilePath @Arguments

  if ($LASTEXITCODE -ne 0) {
    $argText = $Arguments -join " "
    throw ("Command failed with exit code " + $LASTEXITCODE + ": " + $FilePath + " " + $argText)
  }
}

from pathlib import Path
import json
import re
from datetime import datetime, timezone

version_path = Path("VERSION")
manifest_path = Path("extension/manifest.json")
content_path = Path("extension/content_script.js")
background_path = Path("extension/background.js")
guide_path = Path("docs/AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_GUIDE.md")

current = version_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8-sig").strip()
m = re.match(r"^(\d+)\.(\d+)\.(\d+)$", current)
if not m:
    raise SystemExit(f"VERSION invalida: {current!r}")

major, minor, patch = map(int, m.groups())

if current == "0.5.50":
    new = "0.5.51"
elif current == "0.5.51":
    new = "0.5.51"
else:
    new = f"{major}.{minor}.{patch + 1}"

tag = f"v{new}-standalone-visible-status-composer-scope"

version_path.write_text(new + "\n", encoding="utf-8")

manifest = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8-sig"))
manifest["version"] = new
manifest["name"] = f"AI Bridge Local {new}"
manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(manifest, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2) + "\n", encoding="utf-8")

content = content_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
background = background_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")

content = re.sub(r'const VERSION = "[^"]+";', f'const VERSION = "{new}";', content)
background = re.sub(r'const VERSION = "[^"]+";', f'const VERSION = "{new}";', background)

for v in ["0.5.51", "0.5.50", "0.5.49", "0.5.48", "0.5.47", "0.5.46", "0.5.45", "0.5.44", "0.5.43", "0.5.42", "0.5.41"]:
    content = content.replace(v, new)
    background = background.replace(v, new)

standalone_marker = "AI Bridge Local: ChatGPT standalone envelope scanner with visible feedback"
if standalone_marker not in content:
    raise SystemExit("Scanner standalone nao encontrado")

head, tail = content.split(standalone_marker, 1)

if "function injectVisibleStatus" not in tail:
    raise SystemExit("injectVisibleStatus nao encontrado no scanner standalone")

if "function findComposer" not in tail:
    raise SystemExit("findComposer nao encontrado no scanner standalone")

helper = r'''
function aiBridgeStandaloneElementVisible(element) {
  if (!element || !(element instanceof Element)) return false;

  const rect = element.getBoundingClientRect();
  const style = getComputedStyle(element);

  return rect.width > 0 &&
    rect.height > 0 &&
    style.visibility !== "hidden" &&
    style.display !== "none";
}

function aiBridgeStandaloneGetText(element) {
  if (!element) return "";
  if ("value" in element) return String(element.value || "");
  return String(element.innerText || element.textContent || "");
}

function aiBridgeStandaloneUsableComposer(element) {
  if (!element || !(element instanceof Element)) return false;
  if (!aiBridgeStandaloneElementVisible(element)) return false;

  const tag = String(element.tagName || "").toUpperCase();
  const type = String(element.getAttribute("type") || "").toLowerCase();
  const id = String(element.id || "").toLowerCase();
  const ariaHidden = String(element.getAttribute("aria-hidden") || "").toLowerCase();
  const disabled = element.disabled || String(element.getAttribute("aria-disabled") || "").toLowerCase() === "true";

  if (disabled) return false;
  if (ariaHidden === "true") return false;
  if (type === "file") return false;
  if (id.includes("upload")) return false;

  if (tag === "TEXTAREA") return true;

  if (tag === "INPUT") {
    return ["", "text", "search"].includes(type);
  }

  if (String(element.getAttribute("contenteditable") || "").toLowerCase() === "true") return true;
  if (String(element.getAttribute("role") || "").toLowerCase() === "textbox") return true;

  return false;
}

function aiBridgeStandaloneDescribeComposerElement(element) {
  if (!element || !(element instanceof Element)) return { found: false };

  return {
    found: true,
    tag: String(element.tagName || ""),
    id: String(element.id || ""),
    role: String(element.getAttribute("role") || ""),
    contenteditable: String(element.getAttribute("contenteditable") || ""),
    testid: String(element.getAttribute("data-testid") || ""),
    aria_label: String(element.getAttribute("aria-label") || ""),
    type: String(element.getAttribute("type") || ""),
    class_name: String(element.className || "").slice(0, 160),
    text_length: aiBridgeStandaloneGetText(element).trim().length
  };
}

function aiBridgeStandaloneFindPreferredComposer() {
  const preferredSelectors = [
    "#prompt-textarea.ProseMirror[contenteditable='true']",
    "div#prompt-textarea[contenteditable='true'][role='textbox']",
    "#prompt-textarea[contenteditable='true']",
    "#prompt-textarea",
    "[data-testid='prompt-textarea']",
    "[aria-label='Converse com o ChatGPT'][contenteditable='true']",
    "[aria-label='Message ChatGPT'][contenteditable='true']",
    "[aria-label='Send a message'][contenteditable='true']",
    "main form .ProseMirror[contenteditable='true']",
    "form .ProseMirror[contenteditable='true']",
    ".ProseMirror[contenteditable='true'][role='textbox']"
  ];

  for (const selector of preferredSelectors) {
    const element = document.querySelector(selector);
    if (aiBridgeStandaloneUsableComposer(element)) return element;
  }

  const fallbackSelectors = [
    "textarea:not([type='file'])",
    "input:not([type='file']):not(#upload-photos):not(#upload-camera)",
    "[contenteditable='true'][role='textbox']",
    "[contenteditable='true']",
    "[role='textbox']"
  ];

  for (const selector of fallbackSelectors) {
    const elements = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(selector));
    for (const element of elements) {
      if (aiBridgeStandaloneUsableComposer(element)) return element;
    }
  }

  return null;
}

'''

if "function aiBridgeStandaloneFindPreferredComposer" not in tail:
    tail = tail.replace("function findComposer() {", helper + "\nfunction findComposer() {", 1)

# Corrige a chamada fora de escopo dentro do standalone.
tail = tail.replace(
    "const aiBridgePreferredComposer = aiBridgeFindChatGptPromptTextarea();",
    "const aiBridgePreferredComposer = aiBridgeStandaloneFindPreferredComposer();"
)

tail = tail.replace(
    'console.log("[Local v" + VERSION + "] using preferred ChatGPT composer", aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(aiBridgePreferredComposer));',
    'console.log("[Local v" + STANDALONE_VERSION + "] standalone using preferred ChatGPT composer", aiBridgeStandaloneDescribeComposerElement(aiBridgePreferredComposer));'
)

tail = tail.replace(
    'console.log("[Local v" + STANDALONE_VERSION + "] using preferred ChatGPT composer", aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(aiBridgePreferredComposer));',
    'console.log("[Local v" + STANDALONE_VERSION + "] standalone using preferred ChatGPT composer", aiBridgeStandaloneDescribeComposerElement(aiBridgePreferredComposer));'
)

# Se restou descriptor fora de escopo dentro do standalone, troca também.
tail = tail.replace(
    "aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(aiBridgePreferredComposer)",
    "aiBridgeStandaloneDescribeComposerElement(aiBridgePreferredComposer)"
)

content = head + standalone_marker + tail

standalone_tail = content.split(standalone_marker, 1)[1]

if "function aiBridgeStandaloneFindPreferredComposer" not in standalone_tail:
    raise SystemExit("Helper standalone de composer nao inserido")

if "const aiBridgePreferredComposer = aiBridgeFindChatGptPromptTextarea();" in standalone_tail:
    raise SystemExit("Scanner standalone ainda chama helper fora de escopo")

if "aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(aiBridgePreferredComposer)" in standalone_tail:
    raise SystemExit("Scanner standalone ainda usa descriptor fora de escopo")

if "standalone using preferred ChatGPT composer" not in standalone_tail:
    raise SystemExit("Log standalone de composer preferido ausente")

if "ChatGPT standalone envelope scanner with visible feedback" not in content:
    raise SystemExit("Scanner standalone ausente apos patch")

if "legacy global body scanner disabled" not in content:
    raise SystemExit("Scanner legado nao parece desativado")

content_path.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8", newline="\n")
background_path.write_text(background, encoding="utf-8", newline="\n")

doc = Path(f"docs/STANDALONE_VISIBLE_STATUS_COMPOSER_SCOPE_{new.replace('.', '')}.md")
doc.write_text(f"""# AI Bridge Local {new} - Standalone visible status composer scope

Data: {datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()}

## Problema

A entrega direta inter-chat funcionou, mas o status visivel no chat origem falhou com:

`aiBridgeFindChatGptPromptTextarea is not defined`

A causa era escopo: o scanner standalone usava helper criado fora do IIFE standalone.

## Correcao

- Adiciona helpers de composer dentro do scanner standalone.
- `findComposer()` do standalone passa a usar `aiBridgeStandaloneFindPreferredComposer()`.
- Prioriza `#prompt-textarea.ProseMirror[contenteditable='true']`.
- Ignora inputs de upload/camera.
- Mantem entrega direta inter-chat ja funcional.
- Mantem gateway obrigatorio para `run-command/local_capability`.
""", encoding="utf-8")

smoke = Path(f"scripts/watcher/smoke_standalone_visible_status_composer_scope_{new.replace('.', '')}.py")
smoke.write_text(r'''from pathlib import Path

bg = Path("extension/background.js").read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")

marker = "AI Bridge Local: ChatGPT standalone envelope scanner with visible feedback"
if marker not in cs:
    raise SystemExit("standalone marker missing")

standalone = cs.split(marker, 1)[1]

required = [
    "function aiBridgeStandaloneFindPreferredComposer",
    "function aiBridgeStandaloneDescribeComposerElement",
    "function aiBridgeStandaloneUsableComposer",
    "#prompt-textarea.ProseMirror[contenteditable='true']",
    "const aiBridgePreferredComposer = aiBridgeStandaloneFindPreferredComposer();",
    "standalone using preferred ChatGPT composer",
    "injectVisibleStatus",
    "directOkStatus",
    "ChatGPT standalone envelope scanner with visible feedback installed",
    "legacy global body scanner disabled",
]

missing = [item for item in required if item not in cs]
if missing:
    raise SystemExit("missing 0.5.51 markers: " + ", ".join(missing))

for forbidden in [
    "const aiBridgePreferredComposer = aiBridgeFindChatGptPromptTextarea();",
    "aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(aiBridgePreferredComposer)",
    "extract(t).forEach(send);",
    "setInterval(sendChatHeartbeat,",
    'aiBridgeSafeCallSendChatHeartbeat("direct_call")',
]:
    if forbidden in cs:
        raise SystemExit("forbidden old pattern remains: " + forbidden)

if "mustUseGateway" not in bg or "run-command" not in bg or "local_capability" not in bg:
    raise SystemExit("background gateway safety markers missing")

print("OK smoke_standalone_visible_status_composer_scope")
''', encoding="utf-8")

if guide_path.exists():
    guide = guide_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
    guide = re.sub(r"Versao atual:\s*[0-9]+\.[0-9]+\.[0-9]+", f"Versao atual: {new}", guide)
    guide = re.sub(r"Marco publicado mais recente:\s*.*", f"Marco publicado mais recente: {tag}", guide)

    section = f"## Version alignment {new}"
    if section not in guide:

"""
    guide_path.write_text(guide, encoding="utf-8", newline="\n")

print("OLD_VERSION=" + current)
print("NEW_VERSION=" + new)
print("TAG=" + tag)

  if (!element || !(element instanceof Element)) return false;

  const rect = element.getBoundingClientRect();
  const style = getComputedStyle(element);

  return rect.width > 0 &&
    rect.height > 0 &&

function aiBridgeStandaloneGetText(element) {
  if (!element) return "";
  if ("value" in element) return String(element.value || "");
  return String(element.innerText || element.textContent || "");

function aiBridgeStandaloneUsableComposer(element) {
  if (!element || !(element instanceof Element)) return false;
  if (!aiBridgeStandaloneElementVisible(element)) return false;

  const tag = String(element.tagName || "").toUpperCase();
  const type = String(element.getAttribute("type") || "").toLowerCase();
  const id = String(element.id || "").toLowerCase();
  const ariaHidden = String(element.getAttribute("aria-hidden") || "").toLowerCase();
  const disabled = element.disabled || String(element.getAttribute("aria-disabled") || "").toLowerCase() === "true";

  if (disabled) return false;
  if (ariaHidden === "true") return false;
  if (type === "file") return false;
  if (id.includes("upload")) return false;

  if (tag === "TEXTAREA") return true;

  if (tag === "INPUT") {
    return ["", "text", "search"].includes(type);
  }

  if (String(element.getAttribute("contenteditable") || "").toLowerCase() === "true") return true;
  if (String(element.getAttribute("role") || "").toLowerCase() === "textbox") return true;

  return false;
}

function aiBridgeStandaloneDescribeComposerElement(element) {
  if (!element || !(element instanceof Element)) return { found: false };

  return {
    found: true,
    tag: String(element.tagName || ""),
    id: String(element.id || ""),
    role: String(element.getAttribute("role") || ""),
    contenteditable: String(element.getAttribute("contenteditable") || ""),
    testid: String(element.getAttribute("data-testid") || ""),
    aria_label: String(element.getAttribute("aria-label") || ""),
    type: String(element.getAttribute("type") || ""),
    class_name: String(element.className || "").slice(0, 160),
    text_length: aiBridgeStandaloneGetText(element).trim().length
  };
}

function aiBridgeStandaloneFindPreferredComposer() {
  const preferredSelectors = [
    "#prompt-textarea.ProseMirror[contenteditable='true']",
    "div#prompt-textarea[contenteditable='true'][role='textbox']",
    "#prompt-textarea[contenteditable='true']",
    "#prompt-textarea",
    "[data-testid='prompt-textarea']",
    "[aria-label='Converse com o ChatGPT'][contenteditable='true']",
    "[aria-label='Message ChatGPT'][contenteditable='true']",
    "[aria-label='Send a message'][contenteditable='true']",
    "main form .ProseMirror[contenteditable='true']",
    "form .ProseMirror[contenteditable='true']",
    ".ProseMirror[contenteditable='true'][role='textbox']"
  ];

  for (const selector of preferredSelectors) {
    const element = document.querySelector(selector);
    if (aiBridgeStandaloneUsableComposer(element)) return element;
  }

  const fallbackSelectors = [
    "textarea:not([type='file'])",
    "input:not([type='file']):not(#upload-photos):not(#upload-camera)",
    "[contenteditable='true'][role='textbox']",
    "[contenteditable='true']",
    "[role='textbox']"
  ];

  for (const selector of fallbackSelectors) {
    const elements = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(selector));
    for (const element of elements) {
      if (aiBridgeStandaloneUsableComposer(element)) return element;
    }
  }

  return null;
}

'''

if "function aiBridgeStandaloneFindPreferredComposer" not in tail:
    tail = tail.replace("function findComposer() {", helper + "\nfunction findComposer() {", 1)

tail = tail.replace(
    "const aiBridgePreferredComposer = aiBridgeFindChatGptPromptTextarea();",
    "const aiBridgePreferredComposer = aiBridgeStandaloneFindPreferredComposer();"
)

tail = tail.replace(
    'console.log("[Local v" + VERSION + "] using preferred ChatGPT composer", aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(aiBridgePreferredComposer));',
    'console.log("[Local v" + STANDALONE_VERSION + "] standalone using preferred ChatGPT composer", aiBridgeStandaloneDescribeComposerElement(aiBridgePreferredComposer));'
)

tail = tail.replace(
    'console.log("[Local v" + STANDALONE_VERSION + "] using preferred ChatGPT composer", aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(aiBridgePreferredComposer));',
    'console.log("[Local v" + STANDALONE_VERSION + "] standalone using preferred ChatGPT composer", aiBridgeStandaloneDescribeComposerElement(aiBridgePreferredComposer));'
)

tail = tail.replace(
    "aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(aiBridgePreferredComposer)",
    "aiBridgeStandaloneDescribeComposerElement(aiBridgePreferredComposer)"
)

content = head + standalone_marker + tail
standalone_tail = content.split(standalone_marker, 1)[1]

if "function aiBridgeStandaloneFindPreferredComposer" not in standalone_tail:
    raise SystemExit("helper standalone ausente")
if "const aiBridgePreferredComposer = aiBridgeFindChatGptPromptTextarea();" in standalone_tail:
    raise SystemExit("standalone ainda usa helper fora de escopo")
if "aiBridgeDescribeComposerElement(aiBridgePreferredComposer)" in standalone_tail:
    raise SystemExit("standalone ainda usa descriptor fora de escopo")
if "standalone using preferred ChatGPT composer" not in standalone_tail:
    raise SystemExit("log standalone de composer preferido ausente")
if "legacy global body scanner disabled" not in content:
    raise SystemExit("scanner legado nao parece desativado")

content_path.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8", newline="\n")
background_path.write_text(background, encoding="utf-8", newline="\n")

doc = Path(f"docs/STANDALONE_VISIBLE_STATUS_COMPOSER_SCOPE_{new.replace('.', '')}.md")
doc.write_text(f"""# AI Bridge Local {new} - Standalone visible status composer scope

Data: {datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()}

## Problema

A entrega direta inter-chat funcionou, mas o status visivel no chat origem falhou com:

`aiBridgeFindChatGptPromptTextarea is not defined`

A causa era escopo: o scanner standalone usava helper criado fora do IIFE standalone.

## Correcao

- Adiciona helpers de composer dentro do scanner standalone.
- `findComposer()` do standalone passa a usar `aiBridgeStandaloneFindPreferredComposer()`.
- Prioriza `#prompt-textarea.ProseMirror[contenteditable='true']`.
- Ignora inputs de upload/camera.
- Ajusta o smoke para proibir o helper fora de escopo apenas dentro do standalone.
- Mantem entrega direta inter-chat ja funcional.
- Mantem gateway obrigatorio para `run-command/local_capability`.
""", encoding="utf-8")

smoke = Path(f"scripts/watcher/smoke_standalone_visible_status_composer_scope_{new.replace('.', '')}.py")
smoke.write_text(r'''from pathlib import Path

for forbidden in [

function Invoke-Checked {
  param(
    [Parameter(Mandatory=$true)][string]$FilePath,
    [Parameter(ValueFromRemainingArguments=$true)][string[]]$Arguments
  )

  & $FilePath @Arguments

  if ($LASTEXITCODE -ne 0) {
    $argText = $Arguments -join " "
    throw ("Command failed with exit code " + $LASTEXITCODE + ": " + $FilePath + " " + $argText)
  }
}

$newVersion = (Get-Content VERSION -Raw).Trim()
if ($newVersion -ne "0.5.51") {
  throw "VERSION inesperada: $newVersion. Esperado: 0.5.51"
}

$tag = "v0.5.51-standalone-visible-status-composer-scope"
$doc = "docs/STANDALONE_VISIBLE_STATUS_COMPOSER_SCOPE_0551.md"
$smoke = "scripts/watcher/smoke_standalone_visible_status_composer_scope_0551.py"

# Limpa trailing whitespace nos arquivos alterados do 0.5.51.
$filesToClean = @(
  "VERSION",
  "extension/manifest.json",
  "extension/content_script.js",
  "extension/background.js",
  "docs/AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_GUIDE.md",
  $doc,
  $smoke
)

foreach ($file in $filesToClean) {
  if (Test-Path $file) {
    $text = Get-Content $file -Raw
    $text = $text -replace "[ \t]+(?=\r?\n)", ""
    Set-Content $file $text -NoNewline -Encoding UTF8
  }
}

# Garante newline final em arquivos de texto importantes.
foreach ($file in $filesToClean) {
  if (Test-Path $file) {
    $text = Get-Content $file -Raw
    if (-not $text.EndsWith("`n")) {
      Add-Content $file ""
    }
  }
}

from pathlib import Path
import json
import re
from datetime import datetime, timezone

version_path = Path("VERSION")
manifest_path = Path("extension/manifest.json")
content_path = Path("extension/content_script.js")
background_path = Path("extension/background.js")
guide_path = Path("docs/AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_GUIDE.md")

current = version_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8-sig").strip()

if current in {"0.5.51", "0.5.52"}:
    new = "0.5.52"
else:
    m = re.match(r"^(\d+)\.(\d+)\.(\d+)$", current)
    if not m:
        raise SystemExit(f"VERSION invalida: {current!r}")
    major, minor, patch = map(int, m.groups())
    new = f"{major}.{minor}.{patch + 1}"

tag = f"v{new}-gemini-local-status-prefix-scope"

version_path.write_text(new + "\n", encoding="utf-8")

manifest = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8-sig"))
manifest["version"] = new
manifest["name"] = f"AI Bridge Local {new}"
manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(manifest, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2) + "\n", encoding="utf-8")

content = content_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
background = background_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")

content = re.sub(r'const VERSION = "[^"]+";', f'const VERSION = "{new}";', content)
background = re.sub(r'const VERSION = "[^"]+";', f'const VERSION = "{new}";', background)

for v in ["0.5.52", "0.5.51", "0.5.50", "0.5.49", "0.5.48", "0.5.47", "0.5.46", "0.5.45", "0.5.44", "0.5.43", "0.5.42", "0.5.41"]:
    content = content.replace(v, new)
    background = background.replace(v, new)

prefix_block = '''
var LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES = window.__AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES__ || [
  "[AI_LOCAL_ERRO]",
  "[AI_LOCAL_RUN]",
  "[AI_LOCAL]"
];
window.__AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES__ = LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES;
'''

if "window.__AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES__" not in content:
    if 'const VERSION = "' not in content:
        raise SystemExit("const VERSION nao encontrado em content_script.js")

    content = re.sub(
        r'(const VERSION = "[^"]+";\n)',
        r'\1' + prefix_block + "\n",
        content,
        count=1
    )

if "Gemini envelope observer installed" not in content:
    raise SystemExit("Gemini envelope observer marker ausente")

doc.write_text(f"""# AI Bridge Local {new} - Gemini local status prefix scope

Data: {datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()}

## Problema

O chat Gemini `9b406ec6ce0bcea0` carregou o content script e instalou o Gemini envelope observer, mas o observer quebrou ao chamar `addCandidateText` com:

`LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES is not defined`

## Correcao

- Define `LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES` em escopo global do content script.
- Publica tambem `window.__AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES__`.
- Preserva os prefixos:
  - `[AI_LOCAL_ERRO]`
  - `[AI_LOCAL_RUN]`
  - `[AI_LOCAL]`
- Mantem a rota direta inter-chat sem gateway/DB.
- Mantem gateway obrigatorio para `run-command/local_capability`.

## Validacao esperada

Depois de recarregar a extensao e o Gemini, o console nao deve mais mostrar:

function Invoke-Checked {
  param(
    [Parameter(Mandatory=$true)][string]$FilePath,
    [Parameter(ValueFromRemainingArguments=$true)][string[]]$Arguments
  )

  & $FilePath @Arguments

  if ($LASTEXITCODE -ne 0) {
    $argText = $Arguments -join " "
    throw ("Command failed with exit code " + $LASTEXITCODE + ": " + $FilePath + " " + $argText)
  }
}

from pathlib import Path
import json
import re
from datetime import datetime, timezone

version_path = Path("VERSION")
manifest_path = Path("extension/manifest.json")
content_path = Path("extension/content_script.js")
background_path = Path("extension/background.js")
guide_path = Path("docs/AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_GUIDE.md")

current = version_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8-sig").strip()

if current in {"0.5.51", "0.5.52"}:
    new = "0.5.52"
else:
    m = re.match(r"^(\d+)\.(\d+)\.(\d+)$", current)
    if not m:
        raise SystemExit(f"VERSION invalida: {current!r}")
    major, minor, patch = map(int, m.groups())
    new = f"{major}.{minor}.{patch + 1}"

tag = f"v{new}-gemini-local-status-prefix-scope"

version_path.write_text(new + "\n", encoding="utf-8")

manifest = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8-sig"))
manifest["version"] = new
manifest["name"] = f"AI Bridge Local {new}"
manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(manifest, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2) + "\n", encoding="utf-8")

content = content_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
background = background_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")

content = re.sub(r'const VERSION = "[^"]+";', f'const VERSION = "{new}";', content)
background = re.sub(r'const VERSION = "[^"]+";', f'const VERSION = "{new}";', background)

for v in ["0.5.52", "0.5.51", "0.5.50", "0.5.49", "0.5.48", "0.5.47", "0.5.46", "0.5.45", "0.5.44", "0.5.43", "0.5.42", "0.5.41"]:
    content = content.replace(v, new)
    background = background.replace(v, new)

prefix_block = '''var LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES = globalThis.__AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES__ || [
  "[AI_LOCAL_ERRO]",
  "[AI_LOCAL_RUN]",
  "[AI_LOCAL]"
];
globalThis.__AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES__ = LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES;
window.__AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES__ = LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES;
'''

if "__AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES__" not in content:
    if content.startswith('"use strict";\n'):
        content = content.replace('"use strict";\n', '"use strict";\n' + prefix_block + "\n", 1)
    elif content.startswith("'use strict';\n"):
        content = content.replace("'use strict';\n", "'use strict';\n" + prefix_block + "\n", 1)
    else:
        content = prefix_block + "\n" + content

if "Gemini envelope observer installed" not in content:
    raise SystemExit("Gemini envelope observer marker ausente")

if "LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES" not in content:
    raise SystemExit("LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES ausente apos patch")

if "__AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES__" not in content:
    raise SystemExit("global local status prefixes ausente apos patch")

content_path.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8", newline="\n")
background_path.write_text(background, encoding="utf-8", newline="\n")

doc = Path(f"docs/GEMINI_LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIX_SCOPE_{new.replace('.', '')}.md")
doc.write_text(f"""# AI Bridge Local {new} - Gemini local status prefix scope

Data: {datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()}

## Problema

O Gemini envelope observer quebrava com:

`LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES is not defined`

## Correcao

- Define `LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES` no topo do content script.
- Publica tambem:
  - `globalThis.__AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES__`
  - `window.__AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES__`
- Preserva os prefixos:
  - `[AI_LOCAL_ERRO]`
  - `[AI_LOCAL_RUN]`
  - `[AI_LOCAL]`
- Remove a dependencia de escopo local para o observer do Gemini.
- Mantem rota direta inter-chat sem gateway/DB.
- Mantem gateway obrigatorio para `run-command/local_capability`.

## Validacao esperada

Depois de recarregar a extensao e o Gemini, o console nao deve mais mostrar:

`ReferenceError: LOCAL_STATUS_PREFIXES is not defined`
""", encoding="utf-8")

import re
import json
import subprocess
import sys
from datetime import datetime

ROOT = Path(".")
VERSION_NEW = "0.5.53"
TAG = "v0.5.53-deepseek-outbound-envelope-capture"

content_path = ROOT / "extension" / "content_script.js"
manifest_path = ROOT / "extension" / "manifest.json"
version_path = ROOT / "VERSION"
docs_path = ROOT / "docs" / "DEEPSEEK_OUTBOUND_ENVELOPE_CAPTURE_0553.md"
smoke_path = ROOT / "scripts" / "watcher" / "smoke_deepseek_outbound_envelope_capture_0553.py"

for p in [content_path, manifest_path, version_path]:
    if not p.exists():
        raise SystemExit(f"Arquivo obrigatorio ausente: {p}")

old_version = version_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace").strip()
print(f"OLD_VERSION={old_version}")
print(f"NEW_VERSION={VERSION_NEW}")

content = content_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
manifest = manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")

# 1) Bump version files.
version_path.write_text(VERSION_NEW + "\n", encoding="utf-8")

manifest_obj = json.loads(manifest)
manifest_obj["version"] = VERSION_NEW
manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(manifest_obj, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) + "\n", encoding="utf-8")

content = re.sub(
    r'const VERSION = "[^"]+";',
    f'const VERSION = "{VERSION_NEW}";',
    content,
    count=1
)

# 2) Dedupe source_chat_id_mismatch status injection.
old_mismatch_line = "sendTextToChat(statusText, 'source_chat_id_mismatch_' + (cmd.command_id || 'unknown'));"
new_mismatch_block = """const mismatchKey = 'ai_bridge_source_chat_id_mismatch:' + (cmd.command_id || 'unknown');
try {
  if (sessionStorage.getItem(mismatchKey) === '1') {
    console.warn('[Local v' + VERSION + '] source_chat_id_mismatch suppressed duplicate for', cmd.command_id || 'unknown');
  } else {
    sessionStorage.setItem(mismatchKey, '1');
    sendTextToChat(statusText, 'source_chat_id_mismatch_' + (cmd.command_id || 'unknown'));
  }
} catch (_) {
  sendTextToChat(statusText, 'source_chat_id_mismatch_' + (cmd.command_id || 'unknown'));
}"""
if old_mismatch_line in content and "ai_bridge_source_chat_id_mismatch:" not in content:
    content = content.replace(old_mismatch_line, new_mismatch_block)
    print("PATCHED source_chat_id_mismatch dedupe")
elif "ai_bridge_source_chat_id_mismatch:" in content:
    print("SKIP source_chat_id_mismatch dedupe already present")
else:
    raise SystemExit("Nao encontrei linha source_chat_id_mismatch para patch seguro.")

# 3) Add DeepSeek outbound scanner.
deepseek_block = r'''

/* AI Bridge Local: DeepSeek outbound envelope capture 0.5.53. */
(function installAiBridgeDeepSeekCapturedEnvelopeBridge() {
  if (window.__AI_BRIDGE_DEEPSEEK_CAPTURE_INSTALLED__) return;
  window.__AI_BRIDGE_DEEPSEEK_CAPTURE_INSTALLED__ = true;

  const CAPTURE_VERSION = "0.5.53";
  const START_MARKER = "@@" + "AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_START" + "@@";
  const END_MARKER = "@@" + "AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_END" + "@@";
  const MAX_CAPTURE_CHARS = 30000;
  const DEDUPE_PREFIX = "ai_bridge_deepseek_captured_envelope:";
  const BOOTSTRAP_MS = 2500;
  const bootUntil = Date.now() + BOOTSTRAP_MS;

  function isDeepSeekPage() {
    return /(^|\.)chat\.deepseek\.com$/i.test(location.hostname || "");
  }

  function getDeepSeekChatId() {
    const href = String(location.href || "");
    const match = href.match(/\/a\/chat\/s\/([^/?#]+)/i);
    return match ? decodeURIComponent(match[1]) : "";
  }

  function countOccurrences(haystack, needle) {
    let count = 0;
    let offset = 0;
    while (true) {
      const foundAt = haystack.indexOf(needle, offset);
      if (foundAt < 0) break;
      count += 1;
      offset = foundAt + needle.length;
    }
    return count;
  }

  function extractEnvelopeBlocks(rawText) {
    const text = String(rawText || "");
    if (!text || !text.includes(START_MARKER) || !text.includes(END_MARKER)) return [];
    if (text.length > MAX_CAPTURE_CHARS) return [];

    const blocks = [];
    let offset = 0;
    while (offset < text.length) {
      const start = text.indexOf(START_MARKER, offset);
      if (start < 0) break;
      const bodyStart = start + START_MARKER.length;
      const end = text.indexOf(END_MARKER, bodyStart);
      if (end < 0) break;

      const raw = text.slice(bodyStart, end).trim();
      const rawTextBlock = text.slice(start, end + END_MARKER.length).trim();
      blocks.push({ raw, raw_text: rawTextBlock });
      offset = end + END_MARKER.length;
    }
    return blocks;
  }

  function wasCaptured(commandId) {
    if (!commandId) return true;
    const key = DEDUPE_PREFIX + commandId;
    try {
      if (sessionStorage.getItem(key) === "1") return true;
      sessionStorage.setItem(key, "1");
      return false;
    } catch (_) {
      window.__AI_BRIDGE_DEEPSEEK_CAPTURED_IDS__ = window.__AI_BRIDGE_DEEPSEEK_CAPTURED_IDS__ || new Set();
      if (window.__AI_BRIDGE_DEEPSEEK_CAPTURED_IDS__.has(commandId)) return true;
      window.__AI_BRIDGE_DEEPSEEK_CAPTURED_IDS__.add(commandId);
      return false;
    }
  }

  function isComposerOrInputNode(node) {
    if (!node || !(node instanceof Element)) return false;
    return Boolean(node.closest('textarea,input,[contenteditable="true"],[role="textbox"],form'));
  }

  function parseBlock(block) {
    let envelope;
    try {
      envelope = JSON.parse(block.raw);
    } catch (err) {
      return { ok: false, error: "json_parse_error" };
    }

    if (!envelope || typeof envelope !== "object" || Array.isArray(envelope)) {
      return { ok: false, error: "envelope_not_object" };
    }

    const commandId = String(envelope.command_id || "").trim();
    const sourceChatId = String(envelope.source_chat_id || "").trim();
    const targetChatId = String(envelope.target_chat_id || "").trim();
    const action = String(envelope.action || envelope.type || "").trim();
    const deliveryKind = String(envelope.delivery_kind || "").trim();
    const currentChatId = getDeepSeekChatId();

    if (!commandId) return { ok: false, error: "missing_command_id" };
    if (!currentChatId) return { ok: false, error: "deepseek_chat_id_unknown" };
    if (sourceChatId !== currentChatId) return { ok: false, error: "source_chat_id_mismatch" };
    if (!targetChatId) return { ok: false, error: "missing_target_chat_id" };
    if (action !== "send-chat-message" && action !== "run-command") return { ok: false, error: "action_not_allowed" };
    if (action === "send-chat-message" && deliveryKind !== "inter_agent_message") {
      return { ok: false, error: "send_chat_message_requires_inter_agent_message" };
    }
    if (action === "run-command" && deliveryKind !== "local_capability") {
      return { ok: false, error: "run_command_requires_local_capability" };
    }

    return {
      ok: true,
      command_id: commandId,
      envelope,
      raw_text: block.raw_text
    };
  }

  function showNotice(kind, title, detail) {
    try {
      const id = "ai-bridge-deepseek-capture-notice";
      let box = document.getElementById(id);
      if (!box) {
        box = document.createElement("div");
        box.id = id;
        box.style.position = "fixed";
        box.style.zIndex = "2147483647";
        box.style.right = "16px";
        box.style.bottom = "16px";
        box.style.maxWidth = "520px";
        box.style.padding = "10px 12px";
        box.style.borderRadius = "10px";
        box.style.fontFamily = "Arial, sans-serif";
        box.style.fontSize = "12px";
        box.style.lineHeight = "1.35";
        box.style.boxShadow = "0 8px 24px rgba(0,0,0,.24)";
        document.documentElement.appendChild(box);
      }
      box.style.background = kind === "error" ? "#4b1111" : kind === "warn" ? "#4a3608" : "#102a16";
      box.style.color = "#fff";
      box.textContent = title + (detail ? "\n" + detail : "");
      clearTimeout(window.__AI_BRIDGE_DEEPSEEK_CAPTURE_NOTICE_TIMER__);
      window.__AI_BRIDGE_DEEPSEEK_CAPTURE_NOTICE_TIMER__ = setTimeout(() => {
        try { box.remove(); } catch (_) {}
      }, 9000);
    } catch (_) {}
  }

  function sendCapturedEnvelope(parsed) {
    if (wasCaptured(parsed.command_id)) return;

    console.log("[Local v" + CAPTURE_VERSION + "] DeepSeek outbound scanner sending", parsed.command_id);

    chrome.runtime.sendMessage({
      type: "AI_BRIDGE_CAPTURED_ENVELOPE",
      source_chat_id: getDeepSeekChatId(),
      raw_text: parsed.raw_text,
      envelope: parsed.envelope
    }, (response) => {
      const runtimeError = chrome.runtime.lastError;
      if (runtimeError) {
        const msg = runtimeError.message || "runtime_error";
        console.warn("[Local v" + CAPTURE_VERSION + "] DeepSeek captured envelope runtime error:", msg);
        showNotice("error", "[AI_LOCAL_ERRO] DeepSeek watcher local", "id=" + parsed.command_id + "\nerro=" + msg);
        return;
      }

      if (response && response.ok) {
        console.log("[Local v" + CAPTURE_VERSION + "] DeepSeek captured envelope accepted:", parsed.command_id);
        showNotice("success", "[AI_LOCAL] DeepSeek watcher local", "envelope enviado\nid=" + parsed.command_id);
        return;
      }

      const err = response && response.error ? response.error : "background_rejected_captured_envelope";
      console.warn("[Local v" + CAPTURE_VERSION + "] DeepSeek captured envelope rejected:", parsed.command_id, JSON.stringify(response || {}));
      showNotice("error", "[AI_LOCAL_ERRO] DeepSeek watcher local", "id=" + parsed.command_id + "\nerro=" + err);
    });
  }

  function processText(text, reason, bootstrapOnly) {
    const blocks = extractEnvelopeBlocks(text);
    if (!blocks.length) return;

    for (const block of blocks) {
      const parsed = parseBlock(block);
      if (!parsed.ok) continue;

      if (bootstrapOnly || Date.now() < bootUntil) {
        wasCaptured(parsed.command_id);
        continue;
      }

      sendCapturedEnvelope(parsed);
    }
  }

  function scanNode(node, reason, bootstrapOnly) {
    if (!node) return;

    if (node.nodeType === Node.TEXT_NODE) {
      processText(node.textContent || "", reason, bootstrapOnly);
      return;
    }

    if (!(node instanceof Element)) return;
    if (isComposerOrInputNode(node)) return;

    const text = node.innerText || node.textContent || "";
    processText(text, reason, bootstrapOnly);
  }

  function scanDocument(reason, bootstrapOnly) {
    if (!document.body) return;
    scanNode(document.body, reason, bootstrapOnly);
  }

  function installObserver() {
    if (!isDeepSeekPage()) return;
    if (!document.body) return;

    scanDocument("bootstrap", true);

    const observer = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
      for (const mutation of mutations) {
        for (const node of mutation.addedNodes || []) {
          scanNode(node, "mutation", false);
        }
        if (mutation.type === "characterData" && mutation.target) {
          scanNode(mutation.target, "characterData", false);
        }
      }
    });

    observer.observe(document.body, {
      childList: true,
      subtree: true,
      characterData: true
    });

    setTimeout(() => scanDocument("post_bootstrap", false), BOOTSTRAP_MS + 500);
    setInterval(() => scanDocument("interval", false), 5000);

    console.log("[Local v" + CAPTURE_VERSION + "] DeepSeek outbound envelope observer installed for chat:", getDeepSeekChatId());
  }

  if (!isDeepSeekPage()) return;

  if (document.readyState === "loading") {
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", installObserver, { once: true });
  } else {
    installObserver();
  }
})();
'''

if "AI Bridge Local: DeepSeek outbound envelope capture 0.5.53" not in content:
    content = content.rstrip() + "\n" + deepseek_block + "\n"
    print("PATCHED DeepSeek outbound capture")
else:
    print("SKIP DeepSeek outbound capture already present")

content_path.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")

docs_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
docs_path.write_text(f"""# DeepSeek outbound envelope capture 0.5.53

Data: {datetime.now().isoformat()}

## Objetivo

Adicionar captura outbound de envelopes AI Bridge Local no chat.deepseek.com.

## Comportamento esperado

- ChatGPT -> DeepSeek continua usando rota direta ja existente.
- DeepSeek, ao responder com bloco local entre marcadores AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_START e AI_BRIDGE_LOCAL_END, passa a ter o envelope capturado pelo content script.
- O envelope capturado e enviado ao background com type AI_BRIDGE_CAPTURED_ENVELOPE.
- O background valida source_chat_id, action e delivery_kind antes de publicar.
- A aba DeepSeek mostra aviso visual simples de enviado ou erro.
- Envelopes antigos existentes no carregamento inicial sao marcados e nao reenviados.
- source_chat_id_mismatch no ChatGPT fica deduplicado para reduzir ruido quando envelopes de outros chats aparecem colados no historico.

## Validacao manual

1. Recarregar extensao.
2. Recarregar DeepSeek.
3. Confirmar console:
   - DeepSeek outbound envelope observer installed
4. Pedir ao DeepSeek para responder com envelope local.
5. Confirmar aviso visual no DeepSeek:
   - [AI_LOCAL] DeepSeek watcher local
6. Confirmar chegada no chat alvo.
""", encoding="utf-8")

smoke_path.write_text(r'''from pathlib import Path

smoke_path = ROOT / "scripts" / "watcher" / "smoke_deepseek_persistent_delivery_receipt_0554.py"

for p in [content_path, manifest_path, version_path]:
    if not p.exists():
        raise SystemExit(f"Arquivo obrigatorio ausente: {p}")

old_version = version_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace").strip()
print(f"OLD_VERSION={old_version}")
print(f"NEW_VERSION={VERSION_NEW}")
